 donon desh agle paanch varshon main dwipaksheeya vyapaar ko 60 pratishat badhaane ko bhi raji hue
 The two countries agreed to a strategic partnership in the energy sector
 is saajhedaari ke tahat yuai, bharat main petroleum kshetra main shaamil hoga or iske liye tisare deshon se bhi gathjod karegaa
 Prime Minister Narendra Modi and uae's Prince Mohammed bin Zayed Al Nahyan decided to transform india-uae relations into a comprehensive strategic partnership
 saath hi donon netaa yuai main dhanchaagat vikaas main bhartiya companiyon kii bhagidaari ko sugam banane ke liye bhi sahamat hue
 The joint statement issued after the meeting between the two leaders said that the two countries would "further encourage mutual trade and cooperate for this in their regions and outside
" ’’ agle paanch varsh main dwipaksheeya vyapaar main 60 pratishat ke vruddhi ke lakshya ke saath donon deshon ne aarthik sahyog ko vistaar dene kaa nirnay kiya he
 It is noteworthy that in the 1970s, there was an annual turnover of $ 18 million between the two countries, which has now increased to $ 60 billion
 varsh 2014-15 main china or america ke baad yuai, bharat kaa teesraa sabase badha vyapaarik saajhedaar he

 iske liye yuai-bharat dhanchaagat kosh kaa gathan hoga jiskaa lakshya ise 75 arab dollar tak karne kaa rakhaa gaya he

 isse pehle modi ne aaj yuai ke sheersh kaarobaari netaaon ko sambodhit karte hue kaha ki bharat main abhi ek hajaar arab dollar ke nivesh kii kshamta he or unhone yuai ke niveshkon ko bharat main nivesh karne kaa nyauta diya
 In addition, the UAE will use India's expertise in small and medium enterprises to create a diverse industrial base in the UAE

 vinod yadav The agitation of the Jat community, which has been going on for 23 days, demanding the reservation in government jobs in Haryana finally came to an end on Monday
 jat netaaon ne haryana sarkaar ko 13 sitambar tak aarakshan lagu karne kaa samay diya he
 The agitators lifted the blockage from the roads in Hisar district, including National Highway No 10 and other roads and rail tracks
 adhikansh avrodh hisar jile ke mayyar gaanv ke aasapaas kii sadakon par lagaae gaye the
 The agitators ended the agitation and cremated the dead body of Sandeep, a youth killed in police firing
 yuvak kii maut gat mangalvaar ko hui thi
 Jat leader Dharampal Chhot said that the Jat leadership held a meeting with the leaders of various khaps on Monday, in which it was decided to end the agitation
 chhot ne kaha, 'hamen dekhnaa he ki aarakshan kii hamaari maang par haryana sarkaar kya kadam uthaati he
 'know that more than 101 Jat leaders arrested for taking violent forms of reservation movement were released on Sunday evening, yet no announcement was made to end the movement
 reeha kiye gaye 101 jat netaa andolan ke mukhya sthal mayyar gaanv pahunche jahaan unhone agali ranneeti tay karne ke liye baithak kii
 The Bhupendra Singh Hooda government was embarrassed by the non-ending agitation even after the release of Jat leaders, as the state government announced the end of the agitation on Saturday evening after the leaders agreed to demand their release
 darasal, andolankaaree jat netaaon ne shart rakhi thi ki jab tab unke giraftaar netaaon ko reeha nahin kiya jaataa, tab tak ve prashasan or pradesh sarkaar se kisi tarah kii baatcheet nahin karenge
 Life was severely affected for nearly 10 days due to Jat protests in Hisar and adjoining Bhiwani, Jind and Rohtak districts of Haryana
 hisar ko dilli, jind, bhivani or chandigarh se jodne vaale rajmargo ko jam kar die jane or hisar-dilli relpatari avaruddh kiye jane se ensiaar main doodh or sabji utpaadon kii killat ho gai thi
 It is noteworthy that the Jat community has been demonstrating for the last few days the demand for reservation in government jobs under the Other Backward Classes (OBC)
 gat mangalvaar ko police kii golibari main yuvak kii maut se gussaye pradarshnakariyon ne buudhvaar ko dilli jane vaale rashtriya rajmarg or relpatariyon ko jam kar diya tha tathaa ek police stesan ko aag ke hawaale kar diya tha
 Apart from this, a bank branch was also vandalized near Hisar Cantt
 jat netaaon ne aarope lagaaya tha ki mukhyamantri hooda pehle kiye apane vaade se mukar gaye hai or taal-matol kii niti apana rahe hai tathaa andolan ko balpurvak dabaane kaa prayaas kar rahe hai
